/**

 * qualified) or relative.
11 
 *
12 
 * @author Brian Wellington
13 
 */
14

private static final Name wild;

static {

	byteFormat.setMinimumIntegerDigits(3);

	for (int i = 0; i < lowercase.length; i++) {

		if (i < 'A' || i > 'Z')

	empty = new Name();

	wild = new Name();
